Location: Opposite the railway station and the bus passenger transportation center, from the passenger transportation center, adult males can walk at a normal pace within 10 minutes.
Nucleic acid testing is convenient: There is a testing point in the Second People's Hospital in the railway station square, which only provides electronic reports, and the test results will be sent to the mobile phone after 24 hours. Or walk to the opposite bus stop and take bus No. 17 for two stops to the Provincial People's Hospital. The paper report can be obtained after 5:30 pm on the same day after finishing before 10:00 am, and after 9:00 pm on the same day after 10:00 am. It is printed by the printer on the first floor of the emergency center at the rear, which is very convenient for those who leave Xining to stay in this hotel.
Bed: A normal queen size bed with sand pillows and duck down pillows, box spring.
Toilets: 2, one is a manual toilet and the other is an automatic. The light control switch is on the outside.
Bathtub: 1 Bathroom: 1
Steaming room: 1, the temperature can reach 60-65 degrees. I read the reviews before and said that it is broken and can‚Äôt be used, but it is estimated that it will not be used. It is very convenient to click the P button in the lower row of the picture to solve the problem. It takes about 20-30 minutes to reach the temperature of 60 degrees.
Washbasin: 2, one large and the other small in the non-automatic toilet.
Desk: 1 Living room: 1, connected to the living room
TV: 2 sets, supports 4K60FPS screen projection, but it depends on the screen projection capability of your own device. Some devices may be stuck. My mobile phone screen projection at 2K60FPS is very smooth and clear. The picture in the picture may upload lossy but still work. See it is very clear. If you need to hold a small meeting or discussion, you can do a PPT or video projection screen display, which is very convenient.
The curtains are automatic, and the exterior view is a train station. Different rooms may face different directions, and it may be the view from the back. In addition, there are air conditioning buttons at different locations, which can be turned on as appropriate.
Food: Seasonal fruits and nuts will be delivered. If you order breakfast and the front desk says that only halal meals are available, you can order additional meals and they will be delivered to the room in person. It is best to order before 8 pm, and there will be almost no meals at 9 pm. Breakfast is served from 7:30 to 9:00.
Service: When cleaning the room, I will be considerate enough to fold the clothes. If there is additional need, I will know the service staff such as laundry, adding nuts, etc.
Free mineral water provided: 6 bottles, if not enough, you can ask for it.
Toiletries: complete, there is skin care lotion near the sink after bathing.
Soundproofing: very, very good, and the living room and toilet have sliding doors, which are very quiet after they are pulled.
Administrative courtesy: almost none, but the sound insulation is very good, the floor is quiet, and fruits and nuts are given, hoping to enrich this part, which is slightly monotonous.
Points and suggestions that need to be improved: The bathroom needs non-slip shoes, and disposable slippers are really easy to slip and flash to the waist. The service attitude of the food delivery staff still needs to be enthusiastic and feels a little indifferent. Praise the staff at the front desk and door-to-door service. I didn't ask for praise or anything. The service is very good. I want to praise it from the bottom of my heart. However, the front desk does not know about the content that everyone is more concerned about, such as nucleic acid production nearby. It is necessary to enrich the reserves in this area and improve the competitiveness of the hotel. After all, it is important to attract customers to stay after it has actually done a good job.
Gym: The top floor, I didn't go to see it, you can go if you are interested
Wedding banquets can be held, and there are corresponding floors.
Room odor: no smell at all, fresh air. It would be better if there were green plants.
Summary: It is more suitable for business scenarios and guests who need to relieve fatigue.
